 uttar pradesh kii prayagraj loksabhaa seat se bhaajapa saansad shyama charan gupta ne halhi samaajawaadee party kaa daaman thama he

 bataa den, gupta 2014 kaa chunaav bhaajapa ke tikat par lade the or prayagraj se loksabhaa saansad nirvaachit hue the
 In 2004, he won from Banda on a SP ticket
 bataaya jaataa he ki gupta ko is baar bhaajapa dwaara tikat kaate jane kii ashanka thi isliye unhone sapa main jane kaa faisla kiya

 Employees working in the private sector can get a big gift today
 kendriya mantrimandal gracuty bhugtan kanoon (payment of Gratuity Act) ke tahat kar-mukt gracuty seemaa doguni kar 20 lakh rupee karne se jude sanshodhan vidheyak ke masaude par aaj vichaar kar saktaa he
 It has been recommended that people working in the private sector should also get gratuity up to a maximum of Rs 20 lakh, just like central employees
 kanoon main sanshodhan ke baad privet sector amployies 20 lakh rupee tak kii texfri gracuty ke hakdaar ho jaaenge
 The comments pichley dinon shram mantralay kii baithak main privet companiyon ke karmiyon ke naukari chhodane par 10 lakh rupee kii jagah 20 lakh rupee tak gracuty dene par sahmati ban gai thi
 After the proposal is passed by the cabinet, it will be introduced as a bill in Parliament in the next part of the budget session
 dhyaan dilaa den ki saatven vetan ayog ne gracuty kii seemaa das se badhaakar bees lakh karne kii sifarish kii thi jise centre sarkaar or kai rajya sarkarein lagu kar chuki hai
 In a meeting chaired by Labor Minister Bandaru Dattatreya, it was decided to bring such a bill in Parliament that whenever the amount of gratuity of central workers is increased, the gratuity in the private sector also automatically increases
 yah sanshodhan vidheyak aay str main vruddhi ko dekhte hue kanoon main sanshodhan sansad ke bajaae sarkari aadesh ke jariye karne kaa adhikaar centre sarkaar ko dene kii baat kahata he
 Quoting the source, the news agency Bhasha said, "the Union Cabinet may consider the bill related to amendment of gratuity payment law on Wednesday
 ' Recently, in the meeting of the Ministry of Labor, it was agreed to give gratuity up to Rs 20 lakh instead of Rs 10 lakh for the employees of private companies
 cabinet se prastaav paas hone ke baad ise bajet satr ke agle hisse main sansad main vidheyak ke rup main pesh kiya jayega
 It may be noted that the Seventh Pay Commission had recommended raising the limit of gratuity from ten to twenty lakhs, which has been implemented by the Central Government and many State Governments
 shrammantri bandaaru dattatreya kii adhyakshata main hui baithak main faisla liya gaya ki sansad main aisa vidheyak laayaa jaae ki jab bhi kendriyakarmiyon kii gracuty kii raashi main badhotaree hogi to nijee kshetra main bhi gracuty main apane aap ijapha ho
 In view of the increase in the income level, this amendment bill calls for giving the right to the Central Government to amend the law through government order instead of Parliament

 Intolerance and violence betray the spirit of democracy
 ' unhone kaha, 'jo log uttejit karne vaale bhadakaau udgaaron main vishwaas karte hai unhen na to bharat ke mulyon kii or na hi isaki vartmaan raajnneetik man:sthiti kii samaj he
 Indians know that any progress, whether economic or social, is difficult to achieve without peace
 ' These remarks of the President are very important in view of the increase in incidents of communal violence in the country
 mukherjee ne maratha shaasha shivaji kii ore se aurangzeb ko likhe patr kaa ullekh kiya jo unhone tab likhaa tha jab aurangzeb ne jajia lagaaya tha

 ' raashtrapati ne kaha ki asia or africa ke kuch hisson main kattarpanthi ladaakon dwaara dharmik vichaardhaara par aadhaarit bhugolic satta kaayam karne ke liye rashtron ke nakshon ko dobaaraa khinchne ke prayaas kiye ja rahe hai
 Mukherjee said, 'india will feel its repercussions, especially because it represents values that defy every form of terrorism
 bharat loktantr, santulan, antar evam at:dharmik samarasata kii misaal he
 ' raashtrapati ne kaha, 'hamen nishchit taur par puri takat ke saath apane dharmanirpeksh tanebane ko bachaae rakhana he

 ' Referring to good administration, the President said that India needs such creative thinking in governance that helps in speedy development and assures social harmony
 unhone kaha, 'raashtra ko pakshpatpurna udaaegon se upar rakhana hoga

 ' raashtrapati ne kaha ki kisi loktantr main achche prashasan kii shakti kaa prayog rajya kii sansthaaon ke madhyam se samvidhan ke dhaanche ke tahat kiya janaa hota he
